## Coverage Notes

Cambodia's legal database is sourced from two portals:

1. **CDC (cdc.gov.kh)** -- 167 laws with full English PDF text. These are publicly
   downloadable PDFs from the Council for the Development of Cambodia. Full article-level
   provision extraction with 5,876 provisions and 74 definitions.

2. **Camlawbox.com** -- 7,815 legislative entries (laws, sub-decrees, prakas, regulations,
   instructions, notifications). Individual law pages require authentication. These entries
   include title, date, category, and URL metadata. Each is indexed as a single provision
   to enable search and discovery.

## Category Breakdown

| Category | Count | Description |

| sub_decree | 846 | Sub-decrees (Anu-Kret) |
| notification | 807 | Official government notifications |
| act | 746 | Laws (Chbab), codes, constitutional instruments |
| instruction | 371 | Implementation instructions and guidance |
| regulation | 334 | Royal decrees, circulars, regulations |
